Sat Apr 13 11:11:32 UTC 2019
Recompiled programs that require BOOST.
Unfortunately some are not yet compatible and I can't find any patches.

# cd /usr/lib64; for i in libboost_*1.70.0; do ln -s $i ${i%%.*}.so.1.69.0; done
